    // global
    window.SFM_is_mobile = (function () {
        var n = navigator.userAgent;
        var reg = new RegExp('Android\s([0-9\.]*)')
        var match = n.toLowerCase().match(reg);
        var android =  match ? parseFloat(match[1]) : false;
        if (android && android < 3.6) {
        	return;
        };

        return n.match(/Android|BlackBerry|IEMobile|iPhone|iPad|iPod|Opera Mini/i);
    })();

    window.SFM_current_page_menu = '21';

    (function(){

        var mob_bar = '';
        var pos = 'left';
        var iconbar = '';

        var SFM_skew_disabled = ( function( ) {
            var window_width = window.innerWidth;
            var sfm_width = 500;
            if ( sfm_width * 2 >= window_width ) {
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        } )( );

        var classes = SFM_is_mobile ? 'sfm-mobile' : 'sfm-desktop';
        var html = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0]; // pointer
        classes += mob_bar ? ' sfm-mob-nav' : '';
        classes += ' sfm-pos-' + pos;
        classes += iconbar ? ' sfm-bar' : '';
		classes += SFM_skew_disabled ? ' sfm-skew-disabled' : '';

        html.className = html.className == '' ?  classes : html.className + ' ' + classes;

    })();
</script>

<script>

    ;(function (){
        var insertListener = function(event){
            if (event.animationName == "bodyArrived") {
                afterContentArrived();
            }
        }
        var timer, _timer;

        if (document.addEventListener && false) {
            document.addEventListener("animationstart", insertListener, false); // standard + firefox
            document.addEventListener("MSAnimationStart", insertListener, false); // IE
            document.addEventListener("webkitAnimationStart", insertListener, false); // Chrome + Safari
        } else {
            timer = setInterval(function(){
                if (document.body) { //
                    clearInterval(timer);
                    afterContentArrived();
                }
            },14);
        }

        function afterContentArrived() {
            clearTimeout(_timer);
            var htmlClss;

            if ( window.jQuery && window.jQuery.Deferred ) { // additional check bc of Divi theme
                htmlClss = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0].className;
                if (htmlClss.indexOf('sfm-pos') === -1) {
                    document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0].className = htmlClss + ' ' + window.SFM_classes;
                }
                jQuery('body').fadeIn();
                jQuery(document).trigger('sfm_doc_body_arrived');
                window.SFM_EVENT_DISPATCHED = true;
            } else {
                _timer = setTimeout(function(){
                    afterContentArrived();
                },14);
            }
        }
    })()

			<script type="text/javascript">
(function () {
    var header = document.getElementById('ngs-header');
    var body = document.getElementsByTagName('body');

    function throttle(func, wait) {
        let waiting = false;
        return function () {
            if (waiting) {
                return;
            }

            waiting = true;
            setTimeout(() => {
                func.apply(this, arguments);
                waiting = false;
            }, wait);
        };
    }
    function toggleClassName() {
        if (header.classList.contains('elementor-sticky--effects')) {
            body[0].classList.add('scrolling-body');
        } else {
            body[0].classList.remove('scrolling-body');
        }
    }

    window.addEventListener('scroll', throttle((e) => toggleClassName()));
})();
</script>		</div>

                        <span>Ocean</span>
                    </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-title-2472" class="elementor-tab-title elementor-tab-desktop-title  elementor-repeater-item-e3dafe3" data-tab="2" tabindex="2472" role="tab" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2472">

                        <span>Human Histories & Cultures</span>
                    </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-title-2475" class="elementor-tab-title elementor-tab-desktop-title  elementor-repeater-item-47599d7" data-tab="5" tabindex="2475" role="tab" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2475">

                        
                        <span>Planetary Health</span>
                    </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-title-2476" class="elementor-tab-title elementor-tab-desktop-title  elementor-repeater-item-e7fa6f3" data-tab="6" tabindex="2476" role="tab" aria-controls="elementor-tab-content-2476">

                        
                        <span>Space</span>
                    </div>
                            </div>
            <div class="elementor-tabs-content-wrapper">
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-content-2471" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix elementor-active elementor-repeater-item-151f655" data-tab="1" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2471">
                                                    <h5 style="text-align: left;"></h5><h5 style="text-align: left;">Revealing and protecting underwater worlds</h5><p style="text-align: left;">Our Explorers discover, understand, and conserve marine and coastal systems and inspire and empower local and global audiences to better understand and protect the ocean.</p><p style="text-align: left;"><a href="/society/our-focus/ocean/"><u>LEARN MORE</u></a></p>                                            </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-content-2472" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix  elementor-repeater-item-e3dafe3" data-tab="2" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2472">
                                                    <h5 style="text-align: left;"></h5><h5>Preserving and protecting land environments</h5><p style="text-align: left;">Our Explorers explore, understand, and conserve terrestrial and freshwater systems and inspire and empower local and global audiences to better understand and protect our lands, lakes, and rivers.</p><p style="text-align: left;"><a href="/society/our-focus/land/"><u>LEARN MORE</u></a></p>                                            </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-content-2473" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix  elementor-repeater-item-91066ac" data-tab="3" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2473">
                                                    <h5></h5><h5>Protecting and conserving wildlife</h5><p style="text-align: left;">Our Explorers inspire and empower local and global audiences to better understand and protect wildlife, including animals, plants and fungi.</p><p style="text-align: left;"><a href="/society/our-focus/wildlife/"><u>LEARN MORE</u></a></p>                                            </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-content-2474" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix  elementor-repeater-item-041e937" data-tab="4" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2474">
                                                    <h5></h5><h5>Understanding our past and protecting our future</h5><p style="text-align: left;">Our Explorers work to preserve cultural knowledge, better understand human histories, cultures, practices, diversity, and evolutionpast and present, center communities, and inform and inspire global audiences with stories or lessons about humanity.</p><p style="text-align: left;"><a href="/society/our-focus/human-histories-and-cultures/"><u>LEARN MORE</u></a></p>                                            </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-content-2475" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix  elementor-repeater-item-47599d7" data-tab="5" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2475">
                                                    <h5></h5><h5>Protecting the planet</h5><p style="text-align: left;">Our work in Planetary Health covers projects that explore the relationships and interdependencies between human health and the environment. These include all natural systems, such as oceans, land. atmosphere, flora, fauna, fungi and microbes.</p><p style="text-align: left;"><a href="https://www.nationalgeographic.org/society/our-focus/planetary-health/"><u>LEARN MORE</u></a></p>                                            </div>
                                    <div id="elementor-tab-content-2476" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix  elementor-repeater-item-e7fa6f3" data-tab="6" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2476">
                                                    <h5></h5><h5>Exploring what's beyond our world</h5><p style="text-align: left;">Our work in Space encompasses projects dedicated to exploring and understanding the universe and supporting National Geographic Explorers who examine and illuminate our world and what lies beyond it.</p><p style="text-align: left;"><a href="https://www.nationalgeographic.org/society/our-focus/space/"><u>LEARN MORE</u></a></p>                                            </div>

			<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery(window).load(function () {
    const donationTrigger = jQuery('#donation-trigger');
    const donationButton = jQuery('#donation-button .premium-image-button');
    const donationPanel = jQuery('.big-cats .dialog-widget-content');
    
    const popupScript = jQuery('[id="elementor-post-8103-css"]');
    // Hide popup button if the popup is not setup for the page
    if (!popupScript.length) {
        jQuery('#donation-trigger').hide();
    }
    
    if (jQuery('.big-cats').is(':visible')) {
        if (!jQuery('#donation-trigger').hasClass('open-popup')) {
            jQuery('#donation-trigger').addClass('open-popup');
        }
    } 
    
    const isConsentDisplayed = !localStorage.getItem("osano_consentmanager");
    //const hasCookieBanner = jQuery('.osano-cm-window__dialog').is(':visible');
    const topSpacing = !isConsentDisplayed ? 0 : jQuery('.osano-cm-window__dialog').height();
    console.log('topSpacing: ', topSpacing);
    if (!isConsentDisplayed) {
        jQuery('#donation-button .premium-image-button').css('bottom', '20px');
        
        jQuery('.big-cats .dialog-widget-content').css('bottom', '120px');
    }
    
    jQuery(document).on( 'click', '#donation-close', function( event ) {
        elementorProFrontend.modules.popup.closePopup( {id: 8103}, event);
	});
	
	jQuery('#donation-trigger').click(function (event) {
	    if (!jQuery('.big-cats').is(':visible')) {
	        elementorProFrontend.modules.popup.showPopup({id: 8103});
	    } else {
	        jQuery('#donation-trigger').removeClass('open-popup');
	        jQuery('#donation-close').click();
	    }
    });
	
    jQuery(document).on('elementor/popup/show', (event, id, instance) => {
        const isConsentDisplayed = !localStorage.getItem("osano_consentmanager");
        
        if(!isConsentDisplayed) {
            jQuery('.big-cats .dialog-widget-content').css('bottom', '120px');
        } else {
            const topSp = 120;
            jQuery('.big-cats .dialog-widget-content').css('bottom', '' + topSp + 'px');
        }
        
        jQuery('#donation-trigger').addClass('open-popup');
       
    });
    jQuery(document).on('elementor/popup/hide', (event, id, instance) => {
        jQuery('#donation-trigger').removeClass('open-popup');
    });
    
    if (window.Osano) {
        window.Osano('onUiChanged', (component, stateChange) => {
            if (component == 'dialog' && stateChange == 'hide') {
                jQuery('#donation-button .premium-image-button').css('bottom', '20px');
                jQuery('.big-cats .dialog-widget-content').css('bottom', '120px');
            }
        });
    }
});
